Current Commentary

The Issue of Japanese Currency Amidst the Improving Sino-Japanese Trade 23

Sino-Japanese trade has gradually returned to its former state in recent years. By way of example, the Japan Mail Steamship Company transported 345,900 tons of Japanese goods to Shanghai last year, an increase of 65% compared to the 215,430 tons in the previous two years (1933), nearly equivalent to the import volume of the year preceding the Shanghai War (1931). Given the similarities in customs and habits between the two countries, the development of trade should be a natural occurrence. However, the fact that the United States, Britain, and other countries still take precedence in China's foreign trade is attributed by some Japanese to the result of Chinese anti-Japanese sentiment. In our view, this is a flawed interpretation that reverses cause and effect. Chinese industry cannot compete with Japan and relies on the supply of Japanese industrial goods. Furthermore, Japanese goods can be sold at relatively low prices that align with the living standards of the average Chinese person. Japanese merchants also operate in a way that takes into account the convenience of Chinese customers in all aspects, such as setting prices in national currency rather than Japanese currency, which protects Chinese ordering merchants from the risks of exchange rate fluctuations. Their attitude towards people is also not as arrogant as that of Western merchants. Therefore, Chinese people should welcome Japanese goods and have no reason to be hostile towards them. However, the Japanese still do not understand the reasons for the Chinese people's dissatisfaction with Japan and continue to rely on coercion as a means to advance their goals. They may believe that this is the only way to increase exports to China, but they fail to recognize that, in addition to the quality of their goods, stores should also pay attention to the attitude of their staff in treating customers. If they display a "fierce" demeanor, even good products will be avoided. International trade is the same; there is no reason to force people to buy. Now, amidst the gradual improvement of Sino-Japanese trade, Japan continues to maintain its style. For example, the Japanese residents in Shanghai are even trying to further promote the use of Japanese currency, which is truly incomprehensible.

Do Japanese residents not remember that the main customers of industry and commerce in Shanghai are still Chinese? If prices are set in Japanese currency, Chinese people will find it inconvenient to make purchases, and even Japanese stores will have the added burden of temporary currency conversions. If the intention is to avoid losses from Japanese exchange rate fluctuations, this could be considered a valid reason before the exchange rate was stabilized, but in today's era of foreign exchange controls, it is akin to worrying about something that is unlikely to happen. If they intend to circulate old-head tickets in the three northeastern provinces as an example, then it is even more illogical. The circulation of old-head tickets in South Manchuria is similar to the circulation of turnip tickets in North Manchuria, both of which are the result of the excessive issuance of bills and notes in the three provinces. Now that China's currency reform is neither a paper money policy nor inflation, Japanese currency has no chance to take advantage. Moreover, foreign merchant banks in Shanghai have also issued banknotes in Chinese currency, but how many of them are still in circulation today? This shows that although the Chinese are weak, they can love and use their own national currency and will not allow further economic encroachment. It is deeply hoped that the Japanese will abandon their narrow-minded and selfish views and open up today's frustrating situation from a position that benefits both themselves and others. Then, the development of Japanese trade with China will not be difficult to achieve and can leap to the forefront.

Several Officers of the False National Army, Unwilling to Serve the Japanese, Sneak into the Soviet Border and are Imprisoned 32

Moscow - Recently, several officers who defected from the Manchurian army crossed into Soviet territory. The details are as follows: On December 26, a Soviet border patrol detained a non-commissioned officer serving as an adjutant in a Manchurian guard unit near the village of Burutayev, northwest of Soviet territory. He carried a rifle, wore a Japanese military uniform, and was riding a horse near Burutayev and the Chinese village of Luzhuang, infiltrating Soviet territory. He claimed that he was unwilling to serve the Japanese and therefore entered Soviet territory. On December 31, in the Novoyelesiyevka district, one kilometer from the border within Soviet territory, Su Ren, a squad leader of the detachment, was also detained. When they were detained, they stated that the reason for crossing the border was to escape punishment from the Japanese. It is claimed that the Japanese were already aware of their anti-Japanese attitude and anti-Japanese actions. They claimed that they had participated in the intrusion into Soviet territory in the Novoyelesiyev district on December 12. On December 27, a Soviet border patrol detained a Chinese man in the Aigard Nokorsk area. He claimed to be surnamed Liu and named Haihe. He crossed into the Soviet Union from Manchuria. He claimed that he was the commander of the 1st Division of the Northeast People's Army and was conducting anti-Japanese Manchurian military operations. All of the above-mentioned personnel are imprisoned in the usual manner. (TASS dispatch from the 10th)

A Japanese Plane Flies into Russian Territory, Carrying Two Armed Japanese 33

Moscow - Today, a Japanese military plane landed in the Pokrovka district. The location was 30 kilometers northwest of Voroshilov (Nikolsk-Ussuriysk), 35 kilometers from the Soviet border. The plane carried two armed Japanese, one of whom, after landing, immediately walked towards the road. He happened to encounter a farmer driving a cart, whom he tried to stop and force to walk to the landing site of the plane. The farmer fought back, and the result was that the Japanese man was detained. Now he is being transported by cart to Pokrovka. The Japanese man beat the farmer on the road. The two men fought fiercely. The farmer seized a knife from the Japanese man and stabbed him. He then drove the cart towards Pokrovka and pointed out the landing site of the Japanese plane to the border guards along the way. When the border guards were 100 meters from the plane, the other Japanese man opened fire on them. The border guards did not return fire and continued to approach the plane. The Japanese man then fired shots and attacked with a bayonet. The border guards then returned fire, and the Japanese man was wounded. The two wounded Japanese men were both sent to Pokrovka. Voroshilov immediately sent doctors to treat them. The case is currently under serious investigation. (TASS dispatch from the 10th)

Revival of the Anglo-Japanese Alliance 35

Paris - According to a diplomatic correspondent for the newspaper L'Œuvre, some people in the British naval circles are now advocating the restoration of the Anglo-Japanese Alliance, believing that since the United States is mired in an isolationist policy and has failed to advise on Far Eastern affairs, China and Japan can establish a general understanding themselves. Therefore, if the Anglo-Japanese Alliance can be restored, Britain's interests in China can be maintained, and even the position that Britain held in China before the war can be restored. The Naval Conference Will Establish a New Organization; The Five-Power Conference Will Expand to Six Powers 36

If Japan Withdraws, Russia and Germany Will Join; The Conference Will Again Hear the Japanese Representative's Arguments Next Monday; A Qualitative Limitation; Britain and the United States Have in Fact Reached a Compromise

London - The Five-Power Naval Conference will soon become a Six-Power Conference, with Japan withdrawing and Russia and Germany joining. Japan's withdrawal is now a widely recognized fact, but the date has not yet been determined because the Japanese representative, for the sake of prestige, wants to choose the date of withdrawal himself. It will probably be within a few days. The British delegation has accepted the Japanese side's request and decided to ask the conference on Monday to hear Japanese chief delegate Nagano's arguments on the common upper limit. At that time, Nagano will be asked to elaborate on concessions regarding adjustments based on the extent that they do not cause damage. Whether this situation can be extended to Monday depends on the attitude of other delegations. However, judging from the opinions of the delegations, most will announce their opposition to the common upper limit and end this situation. Therefore, the Japanese representative will inevitably withdraw from the conference. As a result, the naval conference will establish a new organization. Quantitative limitation is impossible without Japan's participation. Therefore, it is expected that the conference will focus on the following two points:

Re-discuss the plan for exchanging naval construction procedures in order to eliminate future secret suspicions in the relationship. Begin to implement qualitative restrictions. On this point, the British and American representatives have in fact agreed to limit the tonnage of battleships to 32,000 tons, rather than the 35,000 tons permitted by existing treaties.

It is expected that any agreement reached will contain the hope that Japan can join in the future. However, some delegations now have a feeling that a sliding scale clause should be inserted in the new treaty, so that signatory countries can expand this procedure without restriction when Japan builds ships.

Regarding the possibility of Russia and Germany joining the naval conference, British Secretary of the Admiralty Monsell already mentioned it in the House of Lords last November. Yesterday's talks between the British and Japanese representatives in the Foreign Office have already caused various rumors, but official circles have not acknowledged them. It is reported that British Foreign Secretary Eden, in yesterday's talks, mentioned the text of the Mid-Pacific Defense Project in Washington and hinted at the possibility of Britain building forts in Hong Kong and the United States building forts in the Philippines. (Reuters dispatch from the 10th)

It is reported that the results of the discussions between the British and Japanese chief delegates to the naval conference last night led to the decision to conclude the London Naval Conference. At the plenary session on January 13, the representatives of the five major powers attending will be asked to approve the suspension resolution of the British and Japanese representatives. (Reuters dispatch from the 10th)

As a result of the private consultations between the British and Japanese representatives on the 9th, the British government can, after obtaining the consent of the delegations from the United States, France, and Italy, schedule a discussion on the Japanese proposal for a common maximum limit at the committee meeting on the 13th and intend to adopt it as soon as possible. However, as a result of the adoption, it will be defeated by a four-to-one situation, and the withdrawal of the Japanese delegation will be realized. In fact, the private consultations between Britain and Japan on the 9th have already decided on the general trend of the breakdown of the conference on the Japanese side. However, the Japanese plenipotentiary must request final instructions from the authorities in his home country in advance and intends to report the process and situation of the private consultations between Britain and Japan on the 10th and request instructions separately, so it is necessary to wait quietly for instructions. As for exercising the vote on the 13th, it is intended to avoid it as much as possible, so this vote is often held at the next decision-making meeting. From this point of view, the Japanese plenipotentiary will attend the meeting at most twice. (Domei News Agency dispatch from the 9th)

London - The remaining issue of the disarmament conference, which is on the verge of collapse, is how to conclude the conference in what form. It is expected that the delegates will propose the following declaration to conclude the conference: "Unfortunately, the disarmament conference has failed to reach an agreement and will wait for other opportunities to reconvene the conference. Before this, please countries to be cautious in rebuilding naval competition and strive to maintain friendly relations." (Electric Communication Agency dispatch from the 9th)

Anglo-Japanese Private Talks; Britain is Willing to Accommodate Japan in Order to Leave Room for the Far East Issue 37

London - The Japanese delegation to the naval conference visited the British representatives at the Foreign Office at 4:30 PM today to discuss the situation of the naval conference. The talks ended at 6:30 PM. The spokesperson for the delegation then claimed that the meeting of the General Committee would be postponed. According to what our reporter knows, during today's talks, the Japanese representatives insisted that the quantitative restriction of the navy should be implemented by the common upper limit system and explained to the British representatives that if this issue cannot be resolved in a day, the country cannot continue to participate in all negotiations based on the exchange of naval construction program information. The British representatives replied that the issue of the common upper limit had been repeatedly discussed in the previous meetings, and all parties had exhausted their efforts but to no avail. If it is proposed again now and formally rejected by the countries, the naval conference will inevitably completely fail and must be cautious, etc. The Japanese representatives still insisted on their statement, saying that it is useless to continue negotiations if the issue of quantitative restrictions is not resolved in a day. As a result, Britain reluctantly agreed to change the agenda of the naval conference and re-propose the issue of the common upper limit for discussion, but solemnly stated that Britain's acceptance of this method does not contain the intention of granting naval equality rights to Japan. After the Anglo-Japanese talks were completed, Britain contacted the delegations from the United States, France, and Italy. It was decided that the General Committee would be postponed until Monday of next week, so that the delegations could have ample time to exchange opinions. According to what our reporter learned tonight, the delegations from the United States, France, and Italy will generally accept the change in the agenda. However, they believe that there is no hope of reaching an agreement on the common upper limit system. The American delegation does not want to bear the responsibility for the failure of the naval conference, so it will not oppose the method of changing the conference agenda. However, it is considered that it is unusual for Britain to accept Japan's requirements without any difficulty. In some respects, it is said that Britain is eager to avoid conflicts between Britain and Japan in order to reserve room for resolving various issues in the Far East in the future, so it is willing to accommodate Japan's requirements. According to what our reporter knows, people in British diplomatic circles have already requested the Ministry of the Admiralty to try to avoid a break with Japan, and even if the naval conference unfortunately fails, do not exclude Japan and continue negotiations with the United States, France, and Italy. (Havas dispatch from the 9th)

Eden Hosts US Representative, Explains Reason for Changing Agenda, Four Powers Form Common Front 38

London: Foreign Secretary Eden recently held a banquet at the Carlton Hotel to entertain the U.S. representatives attending the Naval Conference, namely, U.S. Undersecretary of State Norman Davis, along with other U.S. representatives, British representatives, and other dignitaries. It is generally believed that Eden has already informed the U.S. chief representative, Davis, of yesterday's meeting with Japan's Nagano and explained the reasons for Britain's agreement to Japan's request to re-discuss common maximum limits. Regarding Japan's request, which was once shelved years ago, it was rumored that Britain had given the U.S. representatives a promise not to consider it again in the future. The British authorities suddenly agreed yesterday to re-discuss the case, which surprised the U.S. delegation themselves. However, according to information obtained by our reporter, the U.S. delegation will still accept Britain's proposed changes to the agenda, so that the responsibility for the failure of the Naval Conference will be attributed to Japan. People in naval circles believe that Japan's move is due to the trend of Britain, the United States, France, and Italy forming a united front. Therefore, it re-proposed the issue of common maximum limits, hoping to create division. The British government is prepared to deal with this strategy of the Japanese delegation, and the joint method is for Britain, the United States, France, and Italy to jointly respond to Japan's request. The British government has also been in contact with the delegations of the United States, France, and Italy, and has not yet decided whether to temporarily delay or explicitly reject Japan's request. (Havas, 10th)

Alexandria Garrison Holds Simulated Battle Yesterday Morning, Using a Certain European Country as the Hypothetical Enemy 41

Improvement in British-Egyptian Relations 42

Lampson Expresses Willingness to Sign Treaty in Good Faith

Military Alliance to Protect Western Borders is Necessary

Cairo: The leader of the Egyptian National Party is paying closer attention to the actual difficulties due to the Italian-Abyssinian War, so the atmosphere of British-Egyptian relations has now improved. The British representative in Cairo, Miles Lampson, today made a clear statement to the Egyptian government that Britain is willing to sign the 1930 treaty in good faith. However, Lampson made another statement regarding military issues, because according to this treaty, 8,000 British troops are limited to the Canal Zone, which is far from sufficient to protect the western border from sudden attacks. Air attacks are more dangerous than land attacks. Unless Egypt has a sufficient air force, the British Air Force is indispensable for protecting the western border. Lampson also said that the expansion of the Egyptian army requires an expenditure of 15 million pounds and cannot be achieved in a short period of time. Therefore, a British-Egyptian military alliance is necessary for Egypt's own protection. (Reuters, 10th)

Washington: According to statistics announced by the Department of Commerce yesterday, U.S. imports from Shanghai in November 1935 were worth US$1,995,477, compared with US$1,120,108 in November of the previous year. The yuan price in November last year increased by only 12.5 percent compared to November of the previous year, which proves that the quantity and value of some export goods have increased. Mexico Initiates Convening of International Silver Conference, Exploring Attitude of Western Hemisphere Silver-Producing Countries, Difficult to Succeed Without Canada's Participation 45

Washington: It was learned here today that the Mexican government has begun to explore the attitude of Western Hemisphere silver-producing countries towards the International Silver Conference. It is understood that when the finance ministers of Mexico and the United States spoke, the United States expressed its intention to participate. As for whether Mexico has made the same proposal to the third largest silver-producing country in the Western Hemisphere, Canada, it is not yet certain today. However, this conference must have Canada's participation to have any hope of success. The most suitable country to initiate a silver conference is Mexico, because Mexico not only produces the most silver but also occupies a key position in North and South America. Officials at the U.S. State Department are unwilling to discuss this matter, but some Senate silver faction members said that they support this conference and hope that its results can prevent Britain from manipulating the international monetary system with its currency management policies. Some observers believe that although this conference has value, it is extremely difficult to convene, and it requires a great deal of preparation to succeed. However, as a result of current discussions, if it is decided to convene the conference in Mexico City, the United States is willing to participate. Doubts have been expressed here about Canada's attitude due to the recent victory of the Liberal Party. Officials do not know what attitude the Canadian Liberal Party will take towards general silver issues and the silver conference. (National Telegram, 9th)

Hurricane Passes Through England, Uproots Trees, Collapses Houses, Disrupts Transportation 47

London: A hurricane passed through England last night, with speeds reaching 100 miles per hour, causing considerable damage. River levels have risen, threatening to cause flooding. The Lancashire area suffered the most damage. The Manchester police chief broadcast a radio message at night, urging residents to stay indoors and wait for the storm to pass. A small cargo ship broke its anchor in the mouth of the Mersey River, hit a reef, and sank. Only one of the six crew members was rescued. In Lowdham, a large tree was uprooted and crushed two people to death. In Manchester, a girl died due to a wall collapsing. In Leeds, five people were injured when a house collapsed. The famous suspension bridge between Anglesey and Caernarvon is temporarily closed due to a mid-section detachment, but there is no danger of the bridge collapsing. (Reuters, 10th)

London: The hurricane that struck England has caused at least ten deaths and dozens of injuries. The wind speed is 100 miles per hour. A 200-ton cargo ship sank near Formby Point on the Mersey River, drowning ten sailors. Houses were destroyed, roads were damaged, and many towns are out of contact. Ships in the English Channel and flights to and from the mainland have been temporarily suspended. Waves as high as mountains have appeared along the coast, and hundreds of households are in danger of being swept into the sea. The situation of ships at sea is very difficult because the dangerous winds and waves prevent lifeboats from entering the sea. According to the latest news, the Menai Suspension Bridge, the only road to Caernarvon Beach, is shaking violently and may collapse. (National Telegram, 9th)

League of Nations Meeting Approaching, Discussing Oil Embargo Against Italy, Three Reasons Why Britain Will Not Take a Severe Attitude, Eden Will Make Important Speech Before Going to Geneva 48

London: Foreign Secretary Eden will depart for Geneva on January 19 to participate in the League of Nations Council meeting to be held on the 20th. Before departing, he will deliver a speech in his elected district of Leamington on the 17th. This is his first public foreign policy speech since taking office as Foreign Secretary. (Reuters, 9th) The League of Nations Committee of Eighteen is scheduled to meet in Geneva on the 20th of this month to discuss the oil embargo issue. It is unlikely to take a serious decision, or even postpone the decision again. The reason for this is that the U.S. Congress has not yet passed a new neutrality law to give President Roosevelt full power. In addition, even if the Committee of Eighteen wants to make a clear decision on the oil embargo issue, Britain will try to ease it. According to the U.S. proposal, the equal amount of oil exported to Italy in the past five years should be used as the basis to limit the export amount as a compromise. There are several reasons for this: As far as the situation in East Africa is concerned, Mussolini's plan to conquer Abyssinia may fail. However, Britain is still willing to maintain its original power in Europe and make peace with it. Japan's attitude at the Naval Conference is very tough. After the failure of the Naval Conference, its impact will inevitably extend to the Far East issue. Therefore, Britain is cautious about Italy. Germany's rearmament is on a large scale, and the British government has many concerns. In addition, someone rumored yesterday that Sweden intends to propose to the Committee of Eighteen to implement an oil embargo against Italy because Italian aircraft bombed a Swedish rescue team in Abyssinia. Swedish people here have now corrected this, saying that the country does not want to be suspected of retaliation and does not want to propose this method. Although the Soviet Union may propose an oil embargo, the country's ambassador to Britain, Maisky, did not show any signs of acting hastily when he spoke with Foreign Secretary Eden yesterday. From this point of view, the oil embargo issue will not cause major waves. (Havas, 9th)

London: The League of Nations Committee of Eighteen is scheduled to meet on the 20th of this month to discuss the issue of an oil embargo. The U.S. attitude is very important in this matter. Although U.S. President Roosevelt made some announcements in his message to Congress on the 3rd of this month, he did not elaborate. According to the Daily Telegraph, the British and French governments are now planning to inquire about the true meaning of Roosevelt's speech so that they can be well-prepared before the Committee of Eighteen meets and be able to deal with it easily. (Havas, 10th)

Domestic Public Opinion Dissatisfied with New US Neutrality Law 49

New York: Since Representative McReynolds, chairman of the House Foreign Affairs Committee, submitted the new Neutrality Bill to the House on the 3rd of this month, people from all walks of life have criticized it. Harvard University Professor Bowser, originally an authority on international law and consulted by the government, declared that the new Neutrality Bill implements an arms embargo against belligerent countries, regardless of aggressor or victim. As a result, it only helps the strong and suppresses the weak, and the so-called neutrality has become nominal. Bowser also advocated that the United States should invoke the rights of neutral countries to maintain maritime freedom. In addition, Columbia University Professor Hyde also believes that the power granted to the president in this bill is too great. (Havas, 9th)

Total Lunar Eclipse Seen in East Africa, Abyssinian Superstitious Customs 54

Addis Ababa: Our reporter O'Chana reports that during last night's lunar eclipse, the people of the entire city took strange actions, which were very laughable. According to Abyssinian customs, every celestial change is a sign of God's anger, implying that the country is facing a tragedy of bloodshed. During the lunar eclipse, it seems that everyone sees a Jewish lion (the national emblem of Abyssinia) standing upright in the shadow of the moon, glaring fiercely with protruding claws. According to customs, if the situation is favorable to the country, the lion seen must be quiet and peaceful. Last night, groups of people marched in the streets, shouting or singing, and when they arrived in front of the palace, they prayed in unison. When the eclipse lifted and the bright moon was seen in the sky again, order was restored. (Havas, 9th)

During the European War, the Allied Powers Purchased American Arms, Morgan Company Supplied More Than 80% 57

Reuters Special Commercial Report, January 10th

Gold and Silver: London gold price today is 141 shillings exactly, slightly higher by half a penny.

At 10:30 AM, the British-American exchange rate was $4.944375, lower than yesterday's closing rate by 0.0005625. At 1:00 PM, it rose by 0.000125 to $4.945625.

Cotton and Wheat: New York Cotton: Although Liverpool cotton prices fell today, the New York cotton market did not fall at the opening. Instead, there were increases of several points, especially in the near term. The price then soared due to purchases by peers and speculators borrowing under the Bankhead Act to finance cotton purchases. After the price increase, the market stabilized with the January contract price at 5.81, down 11 points.

Liverpool Wheat: The opening today was stable because Australia sold two batches of wheat to the Far East last night. Australian transporters are engaging in hedging to offset this. Although weekly shipments of wheat from around the world to the UK have increased significantly, the amount shipped to Liverpool for resale is not large, so it is still favorable to the bulls. At 1:00 PM, the March contract price rose by half a penny to 6 shillings 5.875 pence. The opening for miscellaneous grains was stable with a slight tendency to recover.

Chicago Wheat: The opening followed the Liverpool market price with a slight increase. The acreage of new wheat fields is still uncertain. Trading is quiet. The opening for miscellaneous grains was lackluster with prices slightly down.

Rubber: London: This morning, the market continued to be stable. At 1:00 PM, the trading price for April and June contracts was 6.8125 pence, 0.0625 higher than yesterday's close.

New York: Because the London market price continued to be firm, the opening also rose by several points. Peers continued to absorb sales, and speculators also bought, so the price continued to rise.

Securities: New York: This morning at the market opening, the prices of various stocks were almost unchanged. Railroad and steel stocks were firmer. Chen Juesheng, Director of the BeiNing Railway Bureau, Deputy Directors Xu Chengyu, Zheng Baozhao, Feng Hewu, Director of the Tianjin Office of the JinPu Railway Bureau, and Deputy Director Zhou Songyao boarded a special train at 7:00 AM and traveled to the Beicang Station to welcome him. Xiao Zhenying, the mayor of Tianjin, made a special trip to the station to greet Zhang. After disembarking, he went to the Palace Hotel on Zhongjie in the British Concession for rest. At 10:30 AM, he was invited by Chen Juesheng to inspect the BeiNing Railway Bureau, touring the various sections of the bureau. Chen gave a speech, and then gathered all the railway staff in the auditorium, inviting Zhang to speak. Zhang said that the BeiNing Line had the longest history among the national railways, and many of the bureau's staff were highly skilled. Since the September 18th Incident, the BeiNing Railway had suffered significant losses, and the environment was very harsh, yet it was still able to operate as usual. He said that the spirit of the employees was admirable and he hoped they would continue with the same spirit, working hard and diligently. Director Chen had been commissioned by Guo Mingling. The Hebei-Chahar Political Council and the Ministry of Railways were both Chinese government entities. The relationship between the BeiNing Railway and the Ministry of Railways remained unchanged. He urged everyone not to easily believe rumors, lest they be misled and it affect their work. After speaking, he left the bureau at 11:00 AM and went to visit the Ningyuan Garden. At 11:30 AM, he made a brief inspection of the Tianjin office of the JinPu Railway Bureau and then went to the Beiran Reception Center at No. 30 in the French Concession to attend a welcoming banquet hosted by Chen Juesheng. In the afternoon at 4:00 PM, the Tianjin banking community held a tea party to welcome him at the Astor Hotel. At 7:00 PM, Xiao Zhenying hosted a dinner at the Dengyinglou Restaurant in the French Concession. At about 8:00 PM, Zhang, along with Shen Chang, Chen Yanjiong, and Chen Juesheng, went to the official residence of the Japanese Army Commander Tada in Zhangyuan, the Japanese Concession, to exchange views on the maintenance of traffic on the eastern section of the BeiNing Railway and the traffic on the various railways in North China. They spoke for about an hour before leaving. At about 6:00 AM on the 8th, he and Shen Chang, Chen Yanjiong, and others took off from the Dongjuzi Airport in Tianjin to meet Han Fuqu in Jinan. After staying for a day, they traveled to Qingdao on the 9th to inspect the Jiaoji Railway, and returned to Jinan on the 10th, before heading south. Inspections of the Zhengtai and Longhai Railways were canceled due to time constraints. The main purpose of Zhang's visit to the north was to meet with Song Zheyuan and Tada in the Tianjin area and to discuss methods to maintain transportation. Regarding the interception of railway funds from the Yutang stations by the pseudo-Eastern Hebei Anti-Communist Autonomous Government, Chen Juesheng was tasked with resolving the diplomatic difficulties and finding ways to stop it. However, it is still undetermined whether this matter will be negotiated separately or resolved as part of the entire Eastern Hebei issue. According to Secretary Yang Jizhi, who accompanied Minister Zhang, during this visit to the north, he visited Suiyuan and Datong, and inspected the PingSui Railway's operations. In the current situation in North China, the transportation of passengers and goods was surprisingly booming, which was truly commendable. The Minister was deeply impressed and sought to increase transportation capacity. The Minister also felt that the personnel arrangements were appropriate. As for how to reorganize the BeiNing Railway administration and the interception of railway funds by the pseudo-XinYu management office, which affected the overall revenue of the railway, the Minister received a telegram from the Ministry today, reporting that the stations east of Tangshan were being held up and the funds were being withheld. The original telegram was forwarded to Director Chen.

Situation in Guangdong's Commercial Market Approaching the Lunar New Year: Poor Performance Across All Sectors, Tight Credit; Request to Government to Improve Commercial Lending Methods 81

Guangzhou Dispatch: With the Lunar New Year approaching, Guangdong's commercial market traditionally settles accounts at the end of the year. However, the past year has been marked by widespread economic downturn and a bleak commercial environment. The situation is particularly dire for real estate and construction companies. Bankruptcies have been reported daily even before the twelfth month. In recent years, Guangzhou's land prices have plummeted, and there is little interest in the properties acquired. As the year ends, funds must be found to repay the debts, but the properties cannot be sold in a timely manner, resulting in numerous bankruptcies and the transfer of assets to creditors. As for the banking sector, commercial banks with strong deposits have benefited greatly from the government's announcement of currency management and the implementation of legal tender last year. Private banks with large cash reserves have also seen profits sufficient to offset losses from the first half of the year. However, most other businesses have seen poor performance and have collected profits in advance. Those who are barely managing feel an extreme shortage of funds. Although the government has recently introduced year-end commercial lending, the interest rates are slightly high and the repayment period is too short, leading to calls for revisions to the lending regulations. Therefore, the Guangzhou Industrial Associations has drafted an opinion and submitted it to the Provincial Government, requesting improvements to the lending methods. The association proposes the following six supplementary measures: 1. The original repayment period is limited to six months. It is proposed to divide it into two types: Type A, with the original six-month term, and Type B, extended by three months to nine months. 2. If borrowers deposit funds in the designated Provincial Bank account during the repayment period for the purpose of repaying the principal upon maturity, the bank should provide a monthly interest rate of 0.6% or 0.5% to show preference. 3. If borrowers sell the mortgaged property before the deadline and repay the loan early, they should be allowed a rebate on the interest at a rate of 0.6% or 0.5% to show special consideration. 4. If multiple businesses with separate licenses mortgage the same property to the Provincial Bank for loans, approval should be granted if the property is deemed adequate, in order to fulfill the purpose of assisting businesses. 5. Businesses that have previously taken out private loans that are about to expire should be allowed to refinance with the Provincial Bank. If the value of the mortgaged property is deemed sufficient, they should be allowed to increase the loan amount. If the mortgage has been transferred to the Land Bureau in accordance with the regulations, and the procedures are clear, re-publication in the newspaper should be waived to avoid complications. 6. For the issuance of Provincial Bank promissory notes, only 50 yuan and 100 yuan denominations should be issued to facilitate commercial transactions and reduce difficulties. It is best to reduce the monthly interest rate on the loan by 0.2% to 0.3%. (January 6)

Guangdong Industrial Bank Established, Total Capital of Five Million Yuan, Commenced Operations on the Sixth of This Month 82

Guangzhou Dispatch: The Guangdong Industrial Bank has been in preparation for several months and was officially established on the fourth of this month. As the new headquarters is under construction, a temporary location has been selected at No. 70, Three-Entrance Alley, Yide Road (the former site of the Ri-Hwa Bank). The bank's operating staff has been transferred from the Municipal Bank. After its opening on the fourth, it was a Saturday holiday, and the following day was also a day of rest, so it officially commenced operations on the sixth. The bank has an authorized capital of five million yuan, jointly operated by the government and private investors. Government shares will be gradually allocated from the Provincial Government's revenue. It focuses on providing loans for provincial factories, land reclamation, water conservancy, and cooperative ventures. The head office is located in Guangzhou, and branch offices or representative offices will be established in counties and cities related to its business. If it is deemed necessary to issue banknotes, it may apply to the government for approval to do so. Of the annual profits, at least one-tenth of the total surplus will be allocated to the public reserve fund, and the remainder will be distributed as dividends to shareholders. Its main business operations include secured loans, with repayment terms ranging from three months to ten years, in installments, fixed terms, and revolving terms, secured by real estate or movable property. The mortgaged property is valued at no more than one-half of its market value, with first mortgages as the principle. Unsecured loans are provided to various cooperatives or public organizations after the bank's investigation confirms their creditworthiness, but the total amount of unsecured loans shall not exceed 10% of the total paid-up capital. Also, overdrafts shall not exceed 10% of the total paid-up capital. Regarding revenue collection, it conducts various savings and deposit operations. Its secondary business includes: Acting as an agent for property purchase, rental collection, and various trusts; Discounting various reliable bills of exchange and promissory notes; Various insurance businesses; and Various remittances. The bank's board of directors consists of 13 members, with 6 official members appointed by the government and the remaining 7 elected by private shareholders. The term of office is temporarily set at three years. The board of directors has five standing directors, elected by the directors from among themselves. The standing directors then elect one person as the chairman to carry out all business operations of the bank. In addition, the bank has one president and one vice president, appointed by the board of directors to handle all matters related to the bank's operations. (January 5)

Overview of the Daokou-Qinghua Railway in the Past Four Years - The Ministry of Railways Has Merged This Railway with the PingHan Railway 83

The Daokou-Qinghua Railway Administration recently released a report on the railway's operations in recent years. According to the report, although the plan to extend the railway line has been completed, it has not been implemented due to difficulty in raising funds. Now, in order to save expenses, the Ministry of Railways has merged this railway with the PingHan Railway, and it is hoped that the future development will be more secure. The report details the organization's activities in the past four years: Income: More than 1.57 million yuan in 1932, more than 1.67 million yuan in 1933, more than 1.79 million yuan in 1934, and more than 1.95 million yuan in 1935, an increase of more than 100,000 yuan each year. Expenditure: More than 1.38 million yuan in 1932, more than 1.44 million yuan in 1933, more than 1.47 million yuan in 1934, and more than 1.49 million yuan in 1935, an average increase of about 30,000 yuan each year. However, in 1921, the maintenance expenses were only more than 160,000 yuan. In 1932, this increased to more than 270,000 yuan, and in 1935, it increased to more than 290,000 yuan. It can be seen that road maintenance engineering is the main reason for the increase in expenditure. Debt Repayment: The railway has two debts, one being the 5% redemption loan, totaling 800,000 British pounds, and the other being the 7% rolling stock loan, totaling 126,838 British pounds 18 shillings 7 pence. Before 1925, principal and interest were paid annually. After 1925, due to the impact of military affairs, the principal and interest were not paid between the years of war. After Director Fan took office, the accumulated surplus from operations was used to repay a total of 24,846 pounds 19 shillings 4 pence in interest on the redemption loan, and a total of 24,384 pounds 9 shillings 1 pence in principal on the rolling stock loan. Negotiations were also held with the creditors to waive compound interest on the rolling stock loan of 16,983 pounds 14 shillings 5 pence, for a total reduction in debt burden of 66,215 pounds 2 shillings 10 pence, equivalent to more than 958,000 yuan in national currency. The Zhongfu Company still owes 600,000 yuan in freight charges this year. After allocating 300,000 yuan for freight charges to other railways, the remaining 300,000 yuan is sufficient to pay one installment of debt interest. Replacement of Sleepers: From 1926 to 1931, only more than 28,000 sleepers were replaced in six years. As of the spring of 1932, the number of damaged sleepers on the entire line reached more than 60%. Since 1932, maintenance expenses have been increased as much as possible. By the end of 1935, a total of more than 113,000 new sleepers had been replaced in four years. The roadbed is stable, and the speed of trains has also gradually increased. Increase in Rolling Stock: At the end of 1931, the railway had 125 freight cars, totaling 3,563 tons. Since 1932, cars scattered on other railways have been gradually recovered, and the Ministry of Railways has allocated new cars, increasing the total number of freight cars by 153, totaling 3,173 tons. The total number of freight cars is now 278, totaling 8,225 tons. In addition, three locomotives and six passenger cars and guard cars have been added. Business Improvement: 1. Passenger fares have been reduced from 1.7 cents per kilometer for third-class tickets to 1.5 cents per 100 kilometers. 2. First and second class passenger transport has been restored. 3. The railway has assumed responsibility for freight transport and joint transport. Savings in Materials: The railway's original material factory was separated from the material section. Since 1933, in order to save expenses and streamline procedures, the material factory has been merged into the material section. A new public system has been established for the purchase of materials, striving to purchase the most practical materials at the lowest prices. In the past four years, the prices of bulk materials such as bituminous coal, wood, and oil have been more than 70% lower compared to the prices of the same materials purchased previously, saving a total of more than 270,000 yuan in material costs. Afforestation Plan: The railway has approximately 340,000 sleepers on the entire line, which need to be replaced every six years. This requires the replacement of 40,000 new sleepers each year. Assuming that one 15-year-old elm tree can be used to make two sleepers, then 20,000 trees must be planted each year so that there will be enough sleepers in 15 years. Since 1932, the railway has been gradually afforesting according to this plan, creating 2,000 hectares of forest land in four years and planting a total of 497,000 trees of various sizes. Expansion Plan: In order to develop business and clear debts, the railway plans to extend the line from Daokou to Damingfu. Over the years, numerous studies have been conducted, and an estimate has been compiled for the extension of the line from Daokou to Damingfu, requiring 3.25 million yuan. In the summer of 1935, a survey team was organized to conduct on-site surveys and draw detailed route maps. Once the funds are raised, construction can begin. Other projects, such as the establishment of a library, an employee club, staff housing, a Daokou-Qinghua public cemetery, and the accumulation of 18,000 yuan in rebates from locomotive coal, are being used for the construction of an auditorium, the opening of a sports field, and the purchase of books. Significant progress has been made on all these fronts. The merger will not undermine the integrity of this railway line.

The Financial Crisis of Militaristic Japan (Part 2) 84

— Huang Fu

Before observing the extraordinary wartime finances, we must first examine the proportion of the so-called military expenditure, which is at the heart of the problem. Tables 1 and 2 illustrate the recent surge in Japan's military expenditure and the enormous size of Japan's military expenditure compared to other imperialist countries in the world.

(From the "Asahi Yearbook," Showa 11th Year, page 153)

From the figures above, we can see that this year's budget (approved by the cabinet) has increased five and a half times compared to 1913, while revenue has only increased by three and nine-tenths. Moreover, the military expenditure mentioned here is limited to the direct expenses under the jurisdiction of the Army and Navy ministries. In addition, indirect military expenses, such as pensions for veterans, annuities, military bond expenses, youth corps training expenses, military education expenses, subsidies for military industries, military national highway expenses, ship improvement subsidies, aviation route construction expenses, expenses related to the Manchurian Incident and the Ministry of Colonial Affairs, etc., if they are also included, then in reality it will "account for more than 80% of the total national budget" ("Social Review," September issue of this year, page 86). The main source of this enormous military expenditure, apart from the aforementioned scraping from the colonies, is deficit public bonds. Here, anyone with economic common sense can understand that a country's issuance of public bonds inevitably has a limit. Exceeding this limit will lead to the danger of malignant inflation or failure to pay public bond interest. In the past four years, Japan's national debt has increased sharply from 5.95 billion yen before September 1931 to 9.202 billion yen in August 1935, a sudden increase of more than 5 billion yen. If we also include the exchange rate difference of foreign debt, the total national debt should be more than 9.76 billion yen. So where did these more than 5 billion yen of public bonds come from? The problem is clear. The agricultural panic of recent years, the poverty of the general public, and the strain on the middle class have caused most of Japan's public bonds to be stored in bank vaults. At the end of 1931, the national debt in bank vaults was 1.811 billion yen, which had increased to 4.146 billion yen by the end of June 1935. In addition, there are 443 million yen of local bonds that have not yet been added.

The situation of the Deposit Bureau is even gloomier. In the past four years, the deposits of the Deposit Bureau have increased by 500 million yen to 3.2 billion yen. However, the national debt and local bonds held by the Deposit Bureau during these four years have surged to the extent shown in the third table:

Table 3: Bonds Held by the Deposit Bureau in the Past Four Years

(National Debt) (Local Debt) Total

September 1931 1,003 (million yen) 590 1,593

June 1935 1,717 950 2,667

In addition to national debt and local bonds, the Deposit Bureau also holds 855 million yen of semi-official enterprise bonds (such as the Hypothec Bank of Japan, the Industrial Bank of Japan, and others). Therefore, the total deposits are 3.2 billion yen, and the amount invested in government securities has reached 3.522 billion yen. In other words, even the reserve funds have been diverted.

The figures quoted above indicate that out of the total of 12.7 billion yen of national debt and local bonds, more than 8 billion yen is fixed in the vaults of financial institutions!

The fact that most of the public bonds are concentrated in financial institutions precisely indicates the narrow digestion capacity of Japan's public bonds and foreshadows that the digestion capacity of public bonds has reached the point of exhaustion. It also clearly illustrates the extent to which Japan's national power depends on financial capital.

The continued issuance of deficit public bonds has been felt to be significantly difficult, while the military expenditure of the "extraordinary times" is still expanding without limit. On the one hand, the agricultural panic has not only not eased but has become increasingly profound. Foreign trade has also gradually slowed down due to the saturation of exchange rate depreciation and the implementation of import restrictions by various countries. Under these strained circumstances, Finance Minister Takahashi, the general agent of the financial world, issued a statement saying, "If credit is destroyed by causing malignant inflation, then national defense cannot be consolidated at that time." From his standpoint, it can be said to be a very natural thing. He said, "It is better to have some preparation and leeway for emergencies." This sentence has a very deep implication. Once Japan goes to war with a foreign country (mainly, of course, the Soviet Union), the current situation is already different from the time of the Russo-Japanese War. The hope of borrowing from abroad is already very slim. Takahashi, who personally borrowed money in London at the time of the Russo-Japanese War, is very clear about this matter.

Two not very harmonious political forces: one is the military, which strongly advocates military adventurism, and the other is the financial capitalists who advocate gradual progress within the scope of national power. The conflict between these two forces has been the center of Japan's domestic political struggle since the London Naval Conference, and it is also the basis of Japan's so-called dual diplomacy. The political situation that unfolds every year with the budget issue as the center is only a superficial phenomenon of the struggle between these two forces.

Now let us take a look at the characteristics of the budget for the coming year (Showa 11th year, 1936). On the one hand, the main policies proposed by the Ministry of Finance are still: 1. Establishing a gradual reduction in deficit public bonds; and 2. Harmonizing national defense spending with general administrative expenses. On the other hand, the military authorities still put forward a request of 1.33 billion yen based on "the military's own view of the world situation." According to the original draft of the Ministry of Finance's budget (November 27th, "Tokyo Asahi Shimbun"), the total revenue for the coming year is 2.238 billion yen, an increase of only 23 million yen compared to this year's 2.215 billion yen (of which deficit public bonds are 666.8 million yen (a decrease of 104.8 million yen compared to this year's 771.6 million yen)); the total expenditure is 2.243 billion yen, of which military expenditure—489 million yen for the army (492 million yen this year) and 539 million yen for the navy (529 million yen this year)—a total of 1.0028 billion yen, already accounts for slightly less than 46 percent of the total expenditure, but it is still more than 310 million yen short of the military's request. As usual, the two military ministers put forward fierce revival requests. After a long period of so-called "political compromise" and a record-breaking all-night, twenty-one-hour cabinet meeting, the claim of "gradual reduction in deficit public bonds" was only superficially implemented, and a budget of 2.271 billion yen, including 1.05 billion yen of military expenditure, was established, unprecedented in Japanese history! The following Table 4 shows the outline of the budget for the coming year:

Table 4: Estimated Budget for Showa 11th Year (Unit: Million Yen)

1. Revenue (Ministry of Finance) (Cabinet Decision Amount) (Increase/Decrease)

Regular Department 1,448 1,450 2 (Increase)

Temporary Department 789 820 31 (Increase)

Including:

Ordinary Revenue 123 141 18 (Increase)

Public Bonds 666 680 14 (Increase)

Total 2,238 2,271 33 (Increase)

2. Expenditure

(Original Draft) (Decision Amount) (Increase/Decrease)

Imperial Household Expenses 45 45 0

Ministry of Foreign Affairs 29 31 2 (Increase)

Ministry of Home Affairs 178 179 1 (Increase)

Ministry of Finance 494 490 4 (Decrease)

Ministry of the Army 489 508 19 (Increase)

Ministry of the Navy 539 551 12 (Increase)

Ministry of Justice 39 39 0

Ministry of Education 141 142 1 (Increase)

Ministry of Agriculture and Forestry 89 90 1 (Increase)

Ministry of Commerce and Industry 16 19 3 (Increase)

Ministry of Communications 195 196 1 (Increase)

Ministry of Colonial Affairs 18 19 1 (Increase)

Total 2,243 2,272 29 (Increase)

From the figures above, we see that the deficit public bonds have been reduced from 770 million yen this year to 660 million yen, and it must be said that the Minister of Finance has implemented the claim of "gradual reduction." However, when we carefully analyze the reasons why public bonds can be gradually reduced, we can know that behind this optimistic "gradual reduction," there are still pessimistic causes hidden, and many artificial manipulations. First, the main reasons for reducing the deficit public bonds in the coming year are the following three: 1. Increased tax revenue; 2. Assistance from special accounts; and 3. The so-called "cooperative budget of various ministries" temporarily pieced together to break the deadlock between the military and financial authorities. Now, let us analyze one by one whether these reasons are solid and whether they have the possibility of continued existence.

Page 10

Hubei Province Actively Carries Out Labor Relief to Repair People's Dikes. 3 Million Public Bonds Pledged for 1.2 Million Yuan. The Flood Relief Association Holds a Special Meeting to Discuss Distribution. 85

Hankou Correspondence: After last year's flood, the authorities discussed relief to address the symptoms with urgent relief and agricultural relief, and to address the root cause with labor relief. Urgent agricultural relief has already been decided and implemented. As for labor relief, from autumn to winter, there has been no solution. The dikes that were breached by the flood in the entire province numbered four to five hundred, and the construction costs required silver tens of millions, which was beyond the ability of the authorities. Later, the Anhui labor plan was adopted, thinking of completing this major task with the service of the people. However, the dike breach areas are the most heavily affected areas. The disaster victims cannot survive without relief. It is not permissible to order complete compulsory service. Therefore, the Flood Relief Association allocated 400,000 yuan from the relief funds donated by various parties and distributed it to 34 cities and counties with the most severe disaster conditions, such as Songzi, Hanchuan, and Hanyang, and designated the most urgent dike repairs to start work first. At the same time, an appeal was made to the central government to subsidize a large amount of relief funds for labor relief. However, because the relief funds were too small, the counties did not distribute them. So far, after a month, no place has started work. The disaster victims are eagerly awaiting relief, still a pie in the sky. On the central government side, the Economic Committee initially reviewed and approved the allocation of 1.5 million yuan of labor relief bonds. A member, Wang Kaihua, was sent by the Flood Relief Association to receive them. The additional 1.5 million yuan of public bonds allocated by the Hubei Central Account Association has not yet been issued. The members of the Flood Relief Association have determined that this money will be used to repair people's dikes for labor relief and have pre-arranged with Finance Director Jia Shiyi to contact the banking syndicate for a pledge. Negotiations have already begun and it is said that 1.2 million yuan can be pledged. It is planned to sign the handover within this month and hand it over to the Flood Relief Association for proper distribution. The Flood Relief Association believes that labor relief is a fundamental work and everything should be carefully planned. A special meeting was specifically convened at 3 pm on the 11th to discuss the progress. It is thought that the labor relief problem, which has been delayed for a long time, will soon be resolved. (8th)

Hunan-Guangxi-Guizhou Troops Encircle Communist Bandits Fleeing in Guizhou. Guangxi Army Units Have Already Arrived at the Guizhou Border. The Border Anti-Bandit Headquarters Will Be Established. 86

Guangzhou Correspondence: The Xiao He Communist bandits have recently been wandering between western Hunan and eastern Guizhou. In the Hongjiang Suining battle at the end of last month, they were pursued by the Hunan army's Fan Fengchi's troops and suffered heavy casualties. A part of the Communist bandits fled to the Guizhou border through Tongdao and took the road to Liping. On the 30th of last month, they fled to Tianzhu and then divided into San Sui Qingxi Jinping to invade. The Guizhou army's Gan Lichu's troops stationed in Qingxi immediately met them head-on and engaged in a fierce battle for three hours. The bandits relied on their strength and stubbornly resisted. On the 31st, another part fled to San Sui, attempting to contain the Guizhou army. Fortunately, the Guizhou army and De Pei's troops stationed there sent teams to outflank the bandits from the rear, resulting in hundreds of bandits killed and prisoners captured. At present, the Guizhou army has not only reinforced its troops to defend its territory but has also telegraphed the Hunan and Guangxi armies to enter the Guizhou border to encircle them. Li Zongren and Bai Chongxi, the commander and deputy commander of the Guangxi army, were recently appointed by the central government as the commander and deputy commander of the Hunan-Guangxi-Guizhou border anti-bandit area. It is said that Li and others consider suppressing bandits and pacifying the people to be the long-cherished aspiration of the Guangxi army and will not shirk their responsibility. They are preparing to set up the anti-bandit headquarters for the Hunan-Guangxi-Guizhou border area near the Fourth Group Army headquarters in Nanning. As for the anti-bandit personnel, they will be concurrently filled by the staff of the Fourth Group Army headquarters to save expenses. It is planned to start work on the 15th of this month. Once the anti-bandit headquarters for the Hunan-Guangxi-Guizhou border area is established, a joint meeting will be telegraphed to the anti-bandit armies of various provinces to send representatives to discuss the overall plan to encircle the Xiao He Communist bandits in the three provinces, so as to fundamentally eliminate them and avoid future troubles. It is expected that the date of the large-scale encirclement by the armies of the three provinces will be realized in the latter half of this month. (January 4th)

Recent Situation in Kulun: The Ruling Authorities Are the Mongolian Youth Faction; Russians Have Freedom of Movement in the Territory. 87

Zhangjiakou Correspondence: Recently, someone who returned to Zhangjiakou from Kulun spoke about the general situation there, stating that after the interruption of transportation between Zhangjiakou and Kulun, trade between the two sides was disrupted and Zhangjiakou was greatly affected, resulting in a depressed scene. As a result, the number of businesses that closed down was countless. Although China and Russia resumed diplomatic relations, there was still no hope of smooth trade and it was mostly manipulated by foreigners. It was difficult to restore the old outlook. Since the tenth year of the Republic of China, the ruling authorities in Kulun have been the Mongolian youth faction, most of whom have studied in Russia. They have made improvements in administration, customs, construction, and education. However, their various measures are mostly imitated from Russia. Regarding transportation, there is a military airfield near Kulun, which is quite large. Groups of airplanes often fly in the sky for training. There are more than three thousand cars in the city, constantly traveling back and forth on the Ri-Cha-Ku (Chakhtu) road, making transportation fairly convenient. The municipal situation has made significant progress compared to before. Buildings are lined up, the roads are flat and clean, and electric lights and telephones are readily available. However, agriculture is not prosperous and there is a shortage of food. The local wheat is black in color and expensive, and the supply cannot meet the demand. If it is transported from Russia and the three northeastern provinces, the distance is long and the freight is high. All other daily necessities rely on external supply, so there is no possibility of reducing the cost of living for the people. As for the thousands of miles of land, they are all pastures, with herds of cattle and sheep in large numbers. The population is mostly Mongolian and Han, followed by Russians. Due to environmental factors, Mongolians and Hans must be proficient in Russian. Hans who operate businesses in the area have mostly become small workers since the tenth year of the Republic of China. They must carry work permits to work, which must be renewed every year. Due to various harsh treatments, many Hans abandon their businesses and take the opportunity to escape secretly. Moreover, Hans entering the country are also strictly prohibited. Therefore, the number of Hans in the area has decreased by more than half compared to ten years ago. However, Russians can come and go as they please and many are workers. This is the recent situation in Kulun.

Anhui Province, Guizhi Dong San Counties: Post-War Reconstruction in the Border Areas, the Province Sends Personnel to Train the Militia Corps 88

Anqing Dispatch: Previously, due to the bandit atmosphere still raging in the border areas of Guichi, Zhide, Dongliu, and other counties in Anhui Province, the provincial government dispatched the Security Director, Hui Ji, to supervise the suppression. Later, Hui reported that the remaining bandits had been completely suppressed and drafted several post-war reconstruction proposals, which were signed and sent to the Provincial Government for review by the Department of Civil Affairs. Now, the Department of Civil Affairs, recognizing the deep and immense suffering of the people in the recovered bandit areas, is actively organizing militia corps to defend them. However, merely organizing without training, lacking knowledge of defense methods and combat, is practically useless. It is proposed that the recovered areas of Guizhi Dong San Counties select two military trainers for each district to specialize in training these militia corps. In addition to military skills, they will also teach general knowledge, ensuring everyone recognizes the correct political path and establishing a foundation for people to enlist in military training. The goal is to achieve effectiveness in two months, and if successful, extend it to neighboring counties and other districts, so that the same education and progress can be achieved, and they can connect with each other as a whole defense plan. Then, the tranquility of the border areas of the three counties can be expected to last permanently. As for these trainers, it is proposed to provide each person with a living allowance of 30 yuan per month. Considering the wider bandit area in Guichi, it is proposed to send four trainers, two to Zhide, and two to Dongliu, requiring a total of eight trainers. The total cost for two months will be 480 yuan. It is proposed that this expense be covered from the anti-banditry funds or the unspent budget for martial arts instructors in the local defense teams of the county. Furthermore, regarding the firearms needed by the militia corps, in addition to each district raising funds to purchase them independently, it is also requested that the Eighth District Special Commissioner be ordered to send all collected discarded firearms to the province for repair, and each district will pay the repair costs to claim and use them. After inspecting the old, discarded Lee-Enfield rifles stored in the Provincial Armory, it was found that 300 of them can still be repaired. Leaving them discarded like this risks decay. If they are issued to the people to guard the blockhouses, it seems that their strength can be slightly increased. It is proposed to repair them all at once, and order each district to pay a certain amount of repair material costs to claim and use them. The gunpowder needed is still abundant in the armory's storage, and it can also be ordered to be purchased in appropriate quantities. The above methods have already been signed and submitted to the Provincial Government for review in a meeting. (January 5th)

Songjiang: Financial Department Committee Member Arrives in Songjiang to Withdraw Funds

Chen Qixiang, a specially appointed secretary of the Department of Finance, arrived in Songjiang in a private car from Shanghai at noon today, to visit the county magistrate. However, the county magistrate was out on official business, and the section chief was also attending a meeting elsewhere, so they did not meet. Secretary Shen Zongliang received him. Changshu: Automobile on the Xihu Road Injures a Person

He Zhangshi, the wife of He Yongfu, a farmer from Zhangjiaba, Hongqiao Township, Second District, went to the city to pay rent at noon on the 6th. While walking along the Yinhu Highway, she was unexpectedly run over and killed by a car heading west from Shanghai near Bridge No. 43 in Guli Village, her head shattered, the scene was extremely tragic. The woman had originally intended to take a boat to the city, but changed her mind to walk due to a headache. Unexpectedly, she became a ghost under the wheels. After the accident, the car fled westward. When the station received the news, the pursuit was too late. According to eyewitnesses, the car was a new streamlined car with paint, Shanghai license number 1136, Beijing Market number 13. After the county government received the report, it sent personnel to the township for inspection on the morning of the 7th, instructing the family to collect the body and wait for the vehicle that caused the accident to be found before further investigation. It is reported that the woman was 47 years old and had a husband and many children at home. She is said to be the first person to die after the opening of the Xihu Highway.

Suzhou: Lake Bandits Continuously Rob Manshan Village

Manshan in Guangfu Township is isolated in the middle of Taihu Lake. The mountain has three villages: Nanshan, Beishan, and Zhongcun, with over 100 households who live by farming. Because the land is located in Taihu Lake and the defenses are weak, theft cases occur from time to time. Unexpectedly, at dawn on the 7th, three bandit boats suddenly arrived at the mountain, carrying more than 30 lake bandits. Their clothes were mixed, some wearing old uniforms, and most held firearms. After climbing the mountain and firing shots as a show of force, they began to rob. Because there were no stationed troops in the township, they did whatever they wanted, searching house by house. It is estimated that they robbed for about two hours, looting a total of seventeen farmhouses in the three villages before leaving, fully loaded. The mountain is quite far from Guangfu Town, so the district office and others did not hear about it until the 10th, when the mountain town office reported it to the district office, which in turn reported it to the county government, requesting the arrest of the bandits. County Magistrate Wu paid close attention to this case. In addition to immediately ordering the security team to rush to search and arrest the lake bandits, he also ordered the Public Security Bureau to have the detective team investigate closely. If there are no clues, a joint suppression will be carried out to maintain security. It was also learned that the Sun family, a farmer living along the edge of Taihu Lake behind Dengwei Mountain in Guangfu Township, was robbed by bandits on the night of the 9th, with minor losses. The bandits escaped into Taihu Lake.

Wuxi: Murderer in Third District Arrested

Chen Agou, a resident of Shenjiawan Township, 64th Tu, Third District, was brutally beaten by his neighbor Chen Afo on April 12th of last year and died from his injuries. At that time, the murderer fled in fear of punishment. The court issued an arrest warrant with a reward of 50 yuan. The reason for Chen Agou's death was that Chen Afo was having an affair with Shen Meisheng's wife, who lived next door. On that day, Chen Afo went to Shen's house for a secret meeting, which was discovered by Chen Agou, who shouted "Catch the adulterer!" As a result, he was severely beaten by Afo and died from his injuries. Recently, Afo, believing that the matter had passed, secretly returned to his hometown. Someone reported this to Zhong Jihe, the captain of the detective team of the Public Security Bureau, requesting his arrest. After receiving the report, Captain Zhong ordered detective Luo Shaoqing to go to the countryside to arrest him the day before yesterday. He successfully arrested Afo and transferred him to the Public Security Bureau. Yesterday, he was transferred to the local court for interrogation.

Changzhou: Wuxi Road to First Operate the Wuxi Section

Since the pawnshops in Wangjiangjing, Nanhui, and other places in Jiaxing were closed, the villagers near Youchegang felt quite inconvenient for pawning and other matters. This was discovered by the Shen family, who intervened with the refugees. However, the refugee leader Zhang Jinhuo refused to intervene and ordered the use of force, with a threatening posture. Even more barbaric refugees used burning rice straw to randomly burn the beams and pillars. It is also learned that the county government has scheduled a meeting of district chiefs at 10:00 AM on the 10th to discuss methods for urging and completing payments. Gaoyou: Long-Distance Bus Overturns into Canal – Ten People Drowned in Unprecedented Tragedy

The Jiangsu Provincial Highway Administration's Qing (Jiang) Yang (Zhou) long-distance bus, passenger car No. Su-1208, left Qingjiang on the 6th. At around 2:00 PM, while traveling on the Yun embankment outside Fengshen Temple Qigong Palace north of this county, the driver was careless, and one of the wheels fell off, causing the car to overturn into the canal, resulting in an unprecedented tragedy. For a time, the whole city was shocked, and over ten thousand people watched. After the accident, 16 passengers (including two women who broke the car windows to escape) were rescued, avoiding the disaster. Later, eight dead passengers were salvaged, and two others were missing. They were carried to Qigong Palace. At around 10:00 AM the day before yesterday, the county government's adjudicator, En Pei, led the coroner and clerk to conduct an inspection and prepared coffins for collection and burial. Li Zhengshu, a staff member of the Second Section of the County Government, was visiting relatives in Huai'an during his annual leave and was returning to Youyou on this bus. He tragically died. The others were surnamed Sun (from Hebei, Huai'an), Jiang Ruizhi, Yin Yisan (both cloth merchants), Zhuang Zian (residing in Lianshui City, former chairman of the Lianshui Chamber of Commerce five years ago), Du Huan (serving in the Tax Police Corps), and the names of the remaining two people are unknown. This car had a total of 26 passengers. Among those who escaped were two assistants from the Sixth Technology Department of the Aviation Committee, one being Yan Mengqin (from Shanghai, 27 years old) and the other being Cheng Yong (from Anhui Province, 30 years old. When escaping, his head hit the car window glass and he suffered abrasions to the head and went to Datong Hospital for treatment, his life is safe). Ma Jingxuan, an employee of the Chinese Education Department of the Shanghai Municipal Council (from Huaiyin, 39 years old), Chen Daoqing, a soldier from the Nanjing Training Headquarters (from Siyang), Fei Xiushan (a businessman from Shiying, 24 years old), and 14 others, as well as two women, one old and one young. After escaping, everyone went to the nearby Tubakou Bathhouse to warm up and change clothes, as their clothes were completely wet. The driver and co-driver of the car, Chuan Xingfa, have been arrested and sent to the county government for handling. In addition to the damage to the car, the clothing and banknotes of the passengers were lost. The wrecked car has been raised out of the water, but has not yet been brought ashore.

Hangzhou: Zhejiang Highway Bureau Implements Austerity

The newly appointed Director of the Highway Bureau, Jiang Jia_, went to the bureau at 9:00 AM on the 10th to take over. Five districts were merged into four districts, and the business offices were merged into one district. Unfinished highway projects, such as the Jiahu Road, Lishan Road, and Yongrui Pingdeng Road, are planned to be continued, and staff will be appropriately reduced to cut expenses. The powers of the management of each district will be increased, and a meeting of the directors of each district will be convened to determine the revenue and expenditure ratio. Performance evaluations will be strictly conducted, and business revenue will be rectified.
